,
{
"@type": "Review",
"reviewRating": {
"@type": "Rating",
"ratingValue": "5"
},
"author": {
"@type": "Person",
"name": "Roy McLean"
},
"reviewBody": "You have to be very careful not to blend the mixture more than you need to. Just gently fold the seasonings into the meat. Gently form the patties. Don't squish them between your hands. You want to preserve the spaces between the bits of ground meat because that is where the juice ends up. If you mix the meat into a smooth homogeneous mass, the juice will run out into the fire."
}

<h2 id="article-subheading_1-0" class="comp type--dog article-subheading">
These burger patties are made with ground beef and an easy bread crumb mixture. Nothing beats a simple hamburger on a warm summer evening. Pile these burgers with your favorite condiments and pop open a cool drink!</h2><!-- end: comp type--dog article-subheading -->

<div id="mntl-recipe-intro_1-0" class="comp mntl-recipe-intro mntl-block">
<div id="mntl-recipe-intro__content_1-0" class="comp mntl-recipe-intro__content mntl-sc-page mntl-block" data-sc-sticky-offset="90" data-sc-ad-label-height="24" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="100" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="4" data-sc-content-positions="[1, 1250, 1550, 1950, 2350, 2750, 3150, 3550, 3950]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Need a basic burger recipe that you can whip up in no time? We have the perfect one. With just 5 ingredients and 15 minutes of cooking time, this flavorful recipe is ready to be shared, topped, and sauced in any way you like! Learn how to make your own sizzling beef burger patties right here.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-1" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-2" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image--no-theme mntl-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">

data-src="https://www.allrecipes.com/thmb/wA8kI4waUaXc6pY_R2GkJDi2YU0=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/25473-the-perfect-basic-burger-ddmfs-4x3-1350-1-f65d5518ecc0435f9791d453ee9cd78f.jpg"

<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-how-to-make-basic-beef-burger-patties"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-3" class="comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> How to Make Basic Beef Burger Patties </span> </h2><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-4" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Nothing says summer quite like a juicy grilled burger. You&#39;ll find the full recipe below with step-by-step instructions, but here&#39;s what you can expect when you make these top-rated burger patties:
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-5" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-6" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Begin by whisking the egg, salt, and pepper together in a large bowl. Then, add the ground beef and bread crumbs before forming the mixture into -inch patties. Place the patties on a preheated grill and cook for six to eight minutes per side.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-7" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-8" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Make sure the beef&#39;s temperature reads at least 160 degrees F before serving, and you&#39;re ready to go. Top with classic condiments like mustard, ketchup, and mayo for full-fledged flavor.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-9" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-how-to-store-beef-burgers"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-10" class="comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> How to Store Beef Burgers </span> </h2><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-11" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Cooked beef burgers can be safely refrigerated for three to four days. Make sure to promptly chill after cooking in an airtight container to lengthen shelf life.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-12" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-can-i-freeze-basic-beef-burgers"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-13" class="comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> Can I Freeze Basic Beef Burgers? </span> </h2><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-14" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Yes, you can freeze cooked burger patties for up to four months. Wrap the burgers in foil individually to discourage sticking before labeling and placing them in a freezer-safe bag.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-15" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-allrecipes-community-tips-and-praise"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-16" class="comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> Allrecipes Community Tips and Praise </span> </h2><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block allrecipes-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-17" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
"We've made these a few times now and the kids love it every time," shares home cook <a href="https://www.allrecipes.com/cook/29461467" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Christel K</a>. "Despite the basic ingredients list it's an absolutely delicious burger, especially when dressed up with some toppings! We add spinach, old cheddar cheese, onions, pickles, plus mustard and mayo."
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-18" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-19" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
"Followed the recipe closely  good hamburgers," says <a href="https://www.allrecipes.com/cook/27660865" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">dwolk</a>. "One note of which to be aware: The recipe calls for 6-8 minutes a side! My ordinary outdoor propane three-burner grill: 3-4 a side and more than medium-rare."
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-20" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-21" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
"Pretty respectable burger, says reviewer<a href="https://www.allrecipes.com/cook/6350270" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1"> berrymoore</a>. "I think I'll add a little onion powder next time to add a little more depth to the flavor."
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-22" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-23" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Editorial contributions by <a href="https://www.allrecipes.com/author/rai-mincey/" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1"><strong>Rai Mincey</strong></a>
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
</div><!-- end: comp mntl-recipe-intro__content mntl-sc-page mntl-block -->
</div><!-- end: comp mntl-recipe-intro mntl-block -->

<div id="mntl-native__adunit_1-0" class="comp scads-to-load mntl-native__adunit mntl-gpt-dynamic-adunit mntl-gpt-adunit gpt native dynamic">
<div id="native" class="wrapper" data-type="native" data-pos="native" data-priority="4" data-sizes="[[1, 3],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-rtb="false" data-wait-for-third-party="false" data-targeting="{}"></div>

<div id="mntl-lrs-ingredients_1-0" class="comp mntl-lrs-ingredients mntl-block" data-load-offset="0" data-vertical-prefix="ar">
<div id="mntl-structured-ingredients_1-0" class="comp mntl-structured-ingredients">
<div class="loc heading">
<h2 id="mntl-structured-ingredients__heading_1-0" class="comp mntl-structured-ingredients__heading mntl-text-block">
Ingredients</h2><!-- end: comp mntl-structured-ingredients__heading mntl-text-block -->
</div>
<ul class="mntl-structured-ingredients__list">
<li
class="mntl-structured-ingredients__list-item "
data-id="16317"
>
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">large</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">egg</span></p>
</li>
<li
class="mntl-structured-ingredients__list-item "
data-id="16421"
>
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true"></span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">teaspoon</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">salt</span></p>
</li>
<li
class="mntl-structured-ingredients__list-item "
data-id="16406"
>
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true"></span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">teaspoon</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">ground black pepper</span></p>
</li>
<li
class="mntl-structured-ingredients__list-item "
data-id="3103"
>
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">pound</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">ground beef</span></p>
</li>
<li
class="mntl-structured-ingredients__list-item "
data-id="2112"
>
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true"></span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">fine dry bread crumbs</span></p>
</li>
</ul>
</div><!-- end: comp mntl-structured-ingredients -->
</div><!-- end: comp mntl-lrs-ingredients mntl-block -->
<div id="recipe__steps_1-0" class="comp recipe__steps mntl-block">
<h2 id="recipe__steps-heading_1-0" class="comp recipe__steps-heading mntl-text-block">
Directions</h2><!-- end: comp recipe__steps-heading mntl-text-block -->
<div id="recipe__steps-content_1-0" class="comp recipe__steps-content mntl-sc-page mntl-block">
<OL id="mntl-sc-block_2-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-group--OL mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup"><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block-group--OL mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup -->
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-1" class="comp mntl-sc-block-group--LI mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup"><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block-group--LI mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-2" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Preheat an outdoor grill for high heat and lightly oil grate.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-3" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-5" class="comp mntl-sc-block-group--LI mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup"><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block-group--LI mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-6" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Whisk together egg, salt, and pepper in a medium bowl. Add ground beef and bread crumbs and mix with your hands or a fork until well blended. Form into four 3/4-inch-thick patties.
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
<div id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-7" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block -->
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-9" class="comp mntl-sc-block-group--LI mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup"><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block-group--LI mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup -->
<p id="mntl-sc-block_2-0-10" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html">
Place patties on the preheated grill. Cover and cook 6 to 8 minutes per side, or to desired doneness. An instant-read thermometer inserted into the center should read at least 160 degrees F (70 degrees C).
</p><!-- end: comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html -->
